The meeting adjourned at 10:30 AM.

External Affairs

Reporting on Recent Diplomatic Situation 63

Yesterday morning (the 20th), the Ministry of Foreign Affairs dispatched Bao Jingan of the Intelligence Department to the Central Broadcasting Station to report on the recent diplomatic situation as follows: "The most important diplomatic news of the past week is summarized as follows: (1) The Sino-Soviet issue is currently a major diplomatic event. Not only is the entire Chinese population paying attention to it, but other countries are also paying close attention to it. Therefore, I will first report on the Sino-Soviet issue. Currently, our representative, Mo Dehui, is still in Moscow conducting informal exchanges of views with the Soviet plenipotentiary representative, Karakhan, in order to seek common ground. This will save many difficulties when the formal meeting opens. The date of the formal meeting has not yet been fully determined. It is regrettable that the Soviet Union is still unwilling to completely release the detained overseas Chinese as the Sino-Soviet conference is about to open. The ministry recently received a telegram from the Consul-General stationed in Vladivostok stating that there are still more than 100 detainees in the Vladivostok area. Most of them have been forcibly charged by the Russian side with disrupting finance, espionage, and counter-revolution, and do not acknowledge that they were arrested because of the Sino-Soviet conflict. In addition, property worth about 200,000 Russian rubles was confiscated during the arrest, and most of it has not been returned. We are currently continuing to strive for their release. After receiving the telegram, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs telegraphed the Consul-General instructing him to continue negotiations. At the same time, it telegraphed the Special Envoy Zhong stationed in Harbin to lodge a serious protest with the Soviet Consul-General stationed in Harbin. In addition, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs received a report from Ju Zengqi, an attaché of the Chinese Embassy in Moscow, stating that many overseas Chinese were arrested after the outbreak of the Sino-Soviet issue and sent to lumber yards in the mountains near Khabarovsk. There are more than 300 Chinese in the mountains who are subjected to various forms of abuse and cannot bear the hardship. More than 200 people were released from Chita after the Sino-Soviet issue was resolved, but more than 100 people have not yet been released. More than 100 overseas Chinese arrested in western Siberia have now been sent to the Mariinsk lumber yard to cut timber. This matter is inconsistent with the previous agreement. Both sides promised that overseas Chinese citizens of both sides arrested for the Sino-Soviet incident after May 1, 1929, would not be categorized and would be released unconditionally. Subsequently, the Chinese authorities immediately released all arrested Russians near Harbin. At the same time, in January of this year, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs also received a telegram from the Chinese Embassy in Germany stating that the German government had received formal notification from the Soviet Ministry of Foreign Affairs that all Chinese citizens arrested throughout the Soviet Union for the Sino-Soviet dispute had been released. According to reports from various sources, the Soviet Union has not fully fulfilled the release of all arrested overseas Chinese, which shows its lack of sincerity. In addition to telegraphing the Special Envoy Zhong stationed in Harbin to lodge a serious protest with the Soviet Consul-General stationed in Harbin, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has telegraphed Representative Mo to quickly question the Soviet representative and ensure the prompt release of all detained overseas Chinese. (2) Protecting overseas Chinese and party affairs. Regarding the protection of overseas Chinese citizens and the elimination of various unequal treatments, the ministry is currently comprehensively planning and proceeding step by step according to a predetermined plan. For countries with treaties, we are striving to negotiate the abolition of old and harsh practices. For countries without treaties, we are conducting separate negotiations to conclude commercial treaties based on the principle of equality and reciprocity to seek fundamental improvement. Regarding the mistreatment of Chinese workers, difficulties in entry, and the levying of exorbitant taxes, we are actively negotiating separately with the countries concerned and are also negotiating revisions to the immigration regulations of various countries, with a view to abolishing discriminatory regulations against overseas Chinese in various countries. Once China's newly concluded treaties of friendship and commerce with various countries are established in order, the treatment of overseas Chinese can gradually be improved. Regarding the British Governor of Singapore's forced dissolution of the party headquarters, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is still actively negotiating. Recently, according to a telegram from Minister Shi stationed in the United Kingdom, the British Foreign Office previously replied that it had not received a report from the British Governor of Singapore and therefore could not handle it. Later, it stated that although the report from the Governor of Singapore had been received, the content was not clear enough and the Colonial Office needed to investigate it in detail before it could reply. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has telegraphed the Minister stationed in the United Kingdom and the Consul-General stationed in Singapore to continue active negotiations. As for the previous report from the South African General Branch stating that the South African Parliament had passed a bill limiting all Chinese merchants operating in South Africa after 1919 to closing their businesses within five years and requesting negotiations, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, upon receiving the news, considered that this matter was of great importance to the lives and property of overseas Chinese and immediately telegraphed the Consul-General stationed in South Africa to inquire. According to reports, the South African Parliament did not discuss this matter during this session, and the report from the South African General Branch may be a misunderstanding. (3) Treaty issues. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs recently received a telegram from Minister Gao Lu stationed in France stating that the instruments of ratification of the Sino-Greek Treaty of Friendship and Commerce were exchanged with the Greek representative at the Chinese Embassy in Paris on the 14th of this month. The original instrument of ratification was sent by mail. The Sino-American Arbitration Treaty was delayed in signing because our country had made some amendments to Article 3 of the treaty. The United States has now accepted our opinion, and the treaty is being translated into French. Once the translation is completed, it can be formally signed. The purpose of this treaty is that if disputes arise between the two contracting countries that cannot be resolved through diplomatic methods, they will be submitted to arbitration, but issues involving the internal affairs of the contracting countries cannot be cited in this treaty. The Sino-Turkish Commercial Treaty has been negotiated several times, and the views of both sides are quite close. The Turkish Chargé d'Affaires Forde will come to Beijing next Monday to continue consultations, and a draft treaty can probably be signed soon. (4) Election of Council Members to the League of Nations. The 11th General Assembly of the League of Nations is scheduled to open in Geneva on September 10. The Council, which presides over the affairs of the conference, is divided into permanent and non-permanent members. The election of non-permanent members is based on the principle of continental representation and is held at each General Assembly. Our country was previously elected as a non-permanent member, but we failed to be re-elected last year. The former Beijing government did not pay much attention to this matter. Since the establishment of the National Government, it has attached great importance to China's position in the international community. Therefore, it is actively seeking to be elected in this year's re-election. To this end, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs telegraphed Ministers Wu, Jiang, and Gao, instructing them to contact the governments of various countries. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has now received telegrams from various ministers reporting on the contact situation. According to a telegram from Minister Gao stationed in France, France has always expressed sympathy for our country and a satisfactory result can be obtained in this re-election. The United Kingdom and Spain have expressed their support. Other countries, such as Czechoslovakia, Siam, Romania, Estonia, Latvia, Yugoslavia, Uruguay, Paraguay, Haiti, and Nicaragua, have also expressed their intention to support China's election. Therefore, China has a good chance of being elected to the Council of the League of Nations this year."

He Yingqin Goes to Hunan to Comfort the Troops 64

A dispatch from Hankou states that after receiving He Jian's report on the recapture of Changsha on the 17th, He Yingqin, Director of the Wuhan Headquarters, immediately telegraphed Commander-in-Chief Chiang to report the victory and planned to personally go to Hunan to comfort the troops and give instructions. On the afternoon of the 18th, he ordered personnel from the Staff Department, Adjutant Department, and Secretariat of the headquarters to prepare to depart with him. At 5:00 PM on the afternoon of the 19th, all important personnel and guards boarded the Wanhua steamer of the Sanbei Company at the riverside wharf. The streets from the headquarters on Huashang Street to the left side of the Sanbei Wharf were guarded by soldiers of the 3rd Regiment of the Military Police with guns. The roads on the right side were guarded by armed soldiers of the Wuhan Garrison Command. The road from the riverbank to the Sanbei pier was patrolled by the Military Police Regiment and the Investigation Team of the Garrison Command, providing strict protection. French Consul Bosde also ordered French sailors stationed in Hankou to land and protect the French Concession, which was extremely thorough. At 6:05 PM, He arrived at the wharf by car from the headquarters. Those accompanying him included Leng Xin, Advisor to the Ministry of Military Affairs; Zhou Weigang, Chief of the Staff Department of the Headquarters; Wang Wenyan, Chief of the Adjutant Department; Liu Jianqun, Director of the Secretariat; Xie Boyuan, Chief of the Confidential Section; Wang Shi, Counselor; and important officers from the Transportation Department, Medical Department, and Accounting Department, as well as a company of guards and all staff of the 9th Radio Station. After shaking hands with the people who came to see him off, He boarded the Wanhua steamer, weighed anchor, and departed. The Desheng warship escorted the steamer. It is reported that after He went to Hunan, the Director of the Wuhan Headquarters will be temporarily replaced by Qian Dajun, Commander of the 3rd Training Division. The duties of the Chief of Staff will be performed by Wang Lun, Deputy Chief of Staff. He is expected to return to Hankou in about a week. (June 20)

Situation of the 4th Route Army Recapturing Changsha 65

A dispatch from Changsha states that the five routes of the Central Army encircled Changsha, and Li Zongren and others abandoned Changsha and retreated to Youxian and Liling, as detailed in previous communications. Early in the morning of the 17th, Wei Suzhong, Deputy Commander of the 15th Division of the 4th Route Army under He Jian, personally led the two regiments of Hou Pengfei and Tian Yingtang, departing from Bairuo Township in Ningxiang County and arriving at the opposite bank of the provincial capital, near Yuelu Mountain, Yingwan City, and the water and land of Shuiluzhou. Li Zongren deployed the Tang Shengming's troops along the riverbank of the province, from Houzi Stone in the upper reaches to Nanhugang in the lower reaches, digging trenches and preparing to defend to the death. The Changsha General Chamber of Commerce sent representatives Zhou Anhan and Wang Zhengshi to negotiate with Tang again and again, asking him to consider the local people and retreat with the Guangxi army and not fight in the provincial capital.

Page 10

Tang initially refused, and then said that his army was mostly composed of Hunan natives and would never be willing to go with the Guangxi army again. He asked representatives Zhou and Wang to convey to Deputy Commander Wei and Regiment Commander Hou, requesting that Commander-in-Chief He allow him to be incorporated and asking the Chamber of Commerce to honor the army's promissory notes of 50,000 yuan in full before he would not fight in Changsha, otherwise he would never withdraw. Zhou and Wang agreed to telegraph the Chamber of Commerce immediately to find a way to raise the money for the promissory notes and stated that the issue of surrender would have to be referred to the authorities. They then consulted Deputy Commander Wei and Regiment Commander Hou on the opposite bank by telephone. Wei and Hou replied at the time that this matter would have to be submitted to Commander-in-Chief He for approval and that Tang's troops must withdraw from Changsha before there could be room for negotiation, and they gave Tang's troops a deadline of 7:00 PM on the 17th to withdraw, and the army decided to cross the river at 8:00 PM. Zhou and Wang negotiated with Tang Shengming again, asking him to withdraw from Changsha temporarily and then discuss it further, but Tang refused. Until 6:00 PM, the Chamber of Commerce had only raised 5,000 yuan for the promissory notes of 50,000 yuan, so Tang Shengming absolutely refused to withdraw. Zhou and Wang were exhausted, but to no avail, and negotiations broke down. At 10:00 PM on the 17th, Deputy Commander Wei, knowing that Tang had no intention of withdrawing, divided his forces into three routes and forced a crossing of the river simultaneously by rowing. Tang Shengming also resisted along the way. The two sides made contact and held each other for about an hour. Regiment Commander Hou had crossed the river and landed from the South Gate. Tang's troops could not hold and fled en masse from Xiaowumen along the Zhuping Road. One part of them was surrounded and disarmed outside Xiaowumen because they could not retreat in time. At 12:00 AM that night, Deputy Commander Wei and Regiment Commanders Hou and Tian entered the city one after another. Tang Shengming frequently told people on the road that his troops were unwilling to cooperate with the Guangxi faction and that he would retreat to Baowu and await reorganization. Early in the morning of the 18th, all stores opened for business and operated as usual, and the city was peaceful as usual. People from all walks of life went to visit Generals Wei, Hou, and Tian to express their condolences and inquire about the military situation. According to Wei and others, his army (Wei Brigade) had encountered only about one enemy camp on its way from Yiyang to the province and had routed it immediately, and there were no traces of the enemy along the way until they made contact when crossing the river in the provincial capital. Commander-in-Chief He is currently in Yiyang and has dispatched a car to welcome him today (the 18th), and he will arrive in the province within days. All circles in the province are now preparing to welcome him. (June 18)

Chen Jitang Departs for Hunan 66

A dispatch from Guangzhou states that the armies from Guangdong, Jiangxi, and Hubei have launched a major encirclement against Zhang and Gui's armies. The Guangdong army's division under Jiang Guangnai has advanced from Hengshan towards the front, and the division under Cai Tingkai has also arrived in Youxian County. The rear division under Li Yangjing has also stationed in Hengshan from Hengyang. Once the Jiangxi's Lu Division arrives at its destination, the order for a general offensive can be issued. Commander-in-Chief of the 8th Route Army Chen Jitang, in order to personally supervise the troops, departed from Guangzhou on the Yuehan train to Shaoguan at 8:00 AM on the 15th and then transferred to Chenzhou. It is understood that those who departed with Chen on that day included Brigade Commander Huang Renhuan, Secretary-General Chen Yukun, and dozens of officers from the headquarters of the 8th Route Army. They arrived in Shaoguan at about 5:00 PM that afternoon. Military and political circles in Shaoguan, having received the telegram in advance, were waiting at the station to greet them. After Chen Jitang got off the train, he rested briefly at the station and was hosted by He Luo, Director of the Military Station; Regiment Commander Fan Dexing; and the Magistrate of Qujiang County. He then went to the headquarters for a rest. It is reported that Chen plans to rest in Shaoguan for one day and depart from Shaoguan for Hunan this morning (the 17th). It is estimated that he will arrive in Chenzhou after the 20th. The First Air Squadron also departed from Shaoguan under the leadership of Huang Guangrui on the 16th. (June 17)

Recent Military News on the Longhai Railway 67

Jin Yun'e Talks About the Situation of Sun's Army in Bozhou

A dispatch from Xuzhou states that, according to reports from the front, in addition to defending the trenches with most of its forces, the enemy on the Longhai Line has also launched attacks on our side with a small number of troops, which have been repelled. Currently, the front-line positions of the two armies are about 40 li apart, and the flanks are about 30 li apart. The two sides on the front line sometimes exchange artillery fire. The deployment of the Central Army has now been finalized, and a general offensive was launched against the enemy on the evening of the 17th. According to news from the railway, after the enemy's defeat, they often use plainclothes teams to gather bandits in an attempt to destroy our line. The railway bureau, in order to prevent this, has long organized an engineering train, led by He Xianhua, Chief of the Engineering Section, to depart for the front. The Jinpu Railway is now also following suit and has sent Deputy Engineer Zhu Weibin to Xuzhou to contact the Transportation Command and establish an engineering train for mobile repairs of the railway line. Currently, the traffic is smooth on the western route from Xuzhou to Minquan, and the rails on the northern route of Dawenkou have also been repaired by the armored train "Beiping" sent by Director He of the Headquarters. Regarding the situation of Sun Dianying's army in Bozhou, Jin Yun'e said that when he arrived near Bozhou City, he saw that the Central Army's forces under Wang and Yang were still besieging the city and could not enter. He had to write a letter himself and send it by plane to the city, advising Sun to pledge his allegiance to the Central Government. The Central Army's forces besieging Bozhou were only a few miles away, and Sun's army was cut off from supplies. Feng Yuxiang and Yan Xishan often used planes to drop flour, cigarettes, and other items into Bozhou from the air, but there were few. Jin has gone to the front this morning (the 19th) to report everything to Chiang. (June 19)

Wuhan Headquarters

Arrest Warrants for Zhao Hengti and Zhang Yinghua 68

Former Hunan Military Governor Zhao Hengti, Minister of Finance Zhang Yinghua, and over ten others have recently secretly arrived in Hankou. They are believed to be residing within the Japanese concession. There are also rumors that Zhao is about to assume the spurious position of Two-Lakes Circuit Commissioner, spreading rumors and creating a tense atmosphere. This matter was discovered by the Hankou municipal Party headquarters. On the 18th, a letter was sent to the military headquarters requesting negotiations with the Japanese consulate for their extradition. In response to the letter, the military headquarters issued an order on the 19th to the Wuhan Garrison Command and the Hankou Municipal Public Security Bureau to issue arrest warrants with rewards. The letter from the municipal Party headquarters and the order from the military headquarters are recorded as follows:

Letter from the Municipal Party Headquarters: It has been secretly reported that over ten individuals, including the remnants of the warlord Zhao Hengti and Zhang Yinghua, recently arrived in Hankou aboard a Japanese ship. They are secretly hiding in the Japanese concession, colluding with reactionary elements, and plotting disturbances. All levels of the municipal Party headquarters and various people's organizations in this city are extremely indignant about this. They have come to the headquarters one after another, requesting serious negotiations with the Japanese consulate and the secret arrest and severe punishment of the traitor Zhao Hengti and others to quell their treacherous schemes. Hankou is located in a vital strategic position, and reactionary elements should not be allowed to disrupt its security. However, the Japanese consulate disregards diplomatic relations and protects the traitorous party, which is deeply regrettable. In addition to sending a letter to the Hankou Special Municipal Government requesting them to lodge a serious protest with the Japanese consulate, we are also sending this letter to your esteemed military headquarters. Please investigate, promptly dispatch a team to secretly arrest Zhao Hengti and his accomplices, and ensure they are severely punished to curb the burgeoning unrest and maintain security. This is a matter of great public importance.

Order from the Military Headquarters Regarding the Issuance of Arrest Warrants with Rewards: It has been found that the two major bandits Zhao Hengti and Zhang Yinghua have long been a scourge to the people. Their crimes are obvious. They have now secretly arrived in Hankou, colluding with vagrants, intending to disrupt social stability and tranquility. Multiple pieces of evidence have been found through repeated investigations, proving their extreme culpability. They must be apprehended immediately to eliminate the traitors. Therefore, this order is issued to the commander, directing all subordinates to conduct strict investigations and arrests. Once they are apprehended, they are authorized to be executed on the spot, without any leniency. Regardless of whether Zhao and Zhang are captured alive or shot dead, a reward of ten thousand yuan will be given for each person apprehended to show encouragement. This order is urgent. (June 20th)

Hubei Construction Department

Plan for Developing Mineral Resources Throughout the Province 69

Establishment of a Mineral Resources Survey Team

Dividing the Province into Seven Major Regions

Hankou Communication: Since the merger of the Agricultural and Mining Department into the Hubei Construction Department, a specialized department has been added to manage agricultural and mining affairs. There are also active plans for development. Hubei Province is rich in mineral resources. In addition to the Daye Iron Mine, which has long been famous both domestically and internationally, coal mines in Yangda, Gui, Yi, and other counties are also being developed by numerous operators. In order to promote the development of the mining industry throughout the province, the department plans to establish a mineral resources survey team, following the example of other provinces, to conduct surveys. The survey area, survey methods, and budget have all been decided, as detailed below:

Survey Area: Based on transportation and geological conditions, the province is divided into seven regions. Region 1: Wuchang, Xianning, Jiayu, Puchai, Chongyang, Tongcheng, Tongshan, Echeng, Daye, Yangxin. Region 2: Huangpi, Huang'an, Macheng, Luotian, Huanggang, Qichun, Qishui, Guangji. Region 3: Xiaogan, Anlu, Yingshan, Yingcheng, Suixian, Zaoyang, Zhongxiang, Jingshan. Region 4: Jingmen, Yuan'an, Dangyang, Yicheng, Xiangyang, Gucheng, Guanghua, Baokang. Region 5: Junxian, Yunxian, Yunxi, Fangxian, Zhushan, Zhuxi. Region 6: Yichang, Xingshan, Zigui, Badong, Changyang, Wufeng, Yidu, Zhijiang, Songzi. Region 7: Hefeng, Xuan'en, Laifeng, Xianfeng, Lichuan, Enshi, Jianshi. Counties that were originally marshlands or have not reported the existence of mines are not included. The survey period for each region is set at three to five months.

Survey Methods: (1) Survey and map the topography of mountains, valleys, rivers, roads, and towns related to mining. (2) Determine the outcrops, strikes, and dips of each mining area and create detailed mineral deposit maps. (3) Create simple geological maps of selected locations passed through. (4) Collect mineral, host rock, and fossil samples. (5) Carry blowpipe analysis equipment to conduct temporary tests. (6) Investigate the area of the mining area, the company organization and its capital, internal and external mining equipment, and transportation methods. (7) Investigate the methods of mining, ventilation, and water drainage in the mine. (8) Investigate the employment system and the source of workers. (9) Investigate the business situation and the source of mining materials. (10) Survey the boundaries of each mining area and create a map of the mining area's relationships. (11) Investigate the annual output, sales market, and current prices. (12) Investigate the education and health facilities for workers and their children. (13) Investigate whether there are any conflicts between labor and management. (14) Investigate whether there are any tax arrears in the mining area.

Survey Expenses: The budget for survey expenses is: (1) Wages: 1224 yuan per year. Item 1: Surveyors, 864 yuan. Item 2: Laborers, 360 yuan. (2) Office Expenses: 2136 yuan. Item 1: Stationery, 204 yuan. Item 2: Printing, 1200 yuan. Item 3: Purchases, 600 yuan. Item 4: Postage and Telecommunications, 96 yuan. (3) Travel Expenses: 5040 yuan. Item 1: Travel expenses for surveyors, 3360 yuan. Item 2: Travel expenses for laborers, 1680 yuan. The total annual expenditure is 8400 yuan. (June 20th)

Local Communications

Jiading 70

Refugees Disturb An Ting Town: On the 17th, a large number of refugees entered the county from Qingpu. The town's defense corps came forward to suppress them, providing relief in the form of over ten yuan in cash and some firewood and rice, which maintained relative stability. The next morning, they marched towards Wangxian Bridge, breaking into farmers' homes along the way and seizing firewood, chickens, ducks, and the like, causing great disturbance to the residents. After arriving in the town, they forcibly occupied schools and temples to live in. The Waigang Public Security Branch and the police team rushed to the scene upon hearing the news, and together with the local defense corps, ordered them to leave the territory. When they refused, after repeated negotiations, the police team hired boats to transport them out of the territory, which was finally completed on the 20th.

Credit Cooperative Provides Agricultural Loans: Because it is now the planting season and members are in great need of funds, the Wucun Credit Cooperative decided at a meeting to borrow 600 yuan from the Jiangsu Provincial Farmers Bank to lend to farmers to provide relief. Loans have already begun to be issued, and members are crowding to borrow due to the convenient procedures and low interest rates.

Qingpu 71

Farmers Bank to Be Established: The county's Farmers Bank fund, which had been levied with the land tax long ago, has accumulated a considerable sum of money. It is currently renting premises on County Front Street to prepare for all aspects of the establishment, and it will soon open. It is rumored that Dai will be the manager.

Complaint Against Standing Committee Member of the Agricultural Consolidation Committee: Zhang Dehua, the former Standing Committee member of the County Agricultural Consolidation Committee, has been reported to the former Provincial Executive Committee by Wang Keming and other staff members of the committee because of his strong personality and near obstinacy. Recently, it was reported that the third district representative assembly of the First District Party Headquarters also submitted a request to the County Party Headquarters to order Zhang Dehua to publish the accounts he handled. It is not known how the County Party Headquarters will handle this.

Songjiang 72

County Party Headquarters Convenes Training Conference: The training department of the county party affairs consolidation committee convened a county-wide training conference on the 21st. Training committee members from each district party headquarters attended. Representatives from each department and office of the committee and representatives from the Education Bureau attended and participated in the discussions. Mi Guangguo, the head of the county training department, presided over the meeting and explained the significance of the meeting, stating that the county-wide training conference is responsible for the overall task of political training and construction, solving all difficult problems in training, and setting the direction for future training work, which is of great significance. Zhu Shouchun, the representative of the Education Bureau, and Yao Qi and Lu Changlin from the county consolidation committee delivered speeches one after another. The training committee members from each district reported on the progress of their work. At 1 PM, the discussion of proposals continued, and after separate deliberation and approval, the meeting adjourned.

Application for Recusal in the Yang Case: In the case of Yang Chen Yunyu, who was previously abused by her husband's sister Yang Ruilan and hid and destroyed her dowry, causing her husband to file for divorce, the case has now been settled by the High Court, and they have reconciled. However, Chen Yunyu filed a criminal lawsuit with the county government, providing evidence from the female servant Gu A'mei and others regarding the abuse by her husband's sister and the destruction of the dowry. Two hearings have been held, and Yang Ruilan was ordered to hand over the original items. Now it is known that Yang Ruilan, while in custody, hired a lawyer to draft an application for recusal and suspension of the case. The county government's ruling stated, "The petition is understood. The application for recusal should be made to the High Court and the previous ruling should be followed. Furthermore, there is no explicit legal provision to suspend proceedings in cases of application for recusal or transfer of jurisdiction. Before a ruling is made in this case, it will be handled personally by the county magistrate."

Suzhou 73

Murderer of Her Own Husband Executed by Hanging: At 7:00 AM yesterday (the 21st), the High Court Prosecutor's Office executed the female prisoner Hu Li by hanging at the Third Sub-Prison. She was 26 years old and from Shengjiazhuang, Xinghua County. She and her husband, Hu Gaoqing, made a living by rowing a boat and collecting grass. The incident occurred on the night of March 21st, 1927, when she and her neighbor, Sheng Qifu (29 years old), were passionately in love and conspired to stab Hu to death with an iron fork and scissors and dumped the body in the river. After the case was uncovered, she was arrested and sent to the county government of that county, where she was sentenced to death. Hu Li and others were not convinced and appealed to the High Court here. After the second instance was rejected, they appealed again. After the third instance, the Supreme Court also ruled that she should be sentenced to death for premeditated murder. The High Court received the execution order and sent Prosecutor Zhu Wenzhuo, accompanied by Clerk Pang Shufeng, to verify her identity and carry out the execution according to law yesterday.

The Defense Corps Seizes Bandits: The Donghoushan Defense Corps seized a bandit ship and three bandits, Liu Dabao, Chen Guangquan, and Chen Genbao, at Xijiao Caozi the day before yesterday (the 19th). They were sent to the city for interrogation yesterday (the 21st).

Investigating the Misappropriation of Public Security Expenses: Yan Yizhuang in Dongting Dongshan was ordered to return the public security expenses collected with the grain tax for 1928, but they have not yet been received to this day, nor has the district office announced the method of disposal. The amount is over 900 yuan, which is somewhat ambiguous. Yesterday (the 21st), they specially submitted a request to the county government for investigation. County Magistrate Huang immediately ordered the district chief, Han Jizhi, to investigate and report on the situation and where the funds are being held.

Deputy Minister of Justice Investigates the Third Sub-Prison: The new warden of the Sima Street Jiangsu Third Sub-Prison, Ding Lei, was accused of abusing his power by transferring thirty untried prisoners, including Chen Yi, Lu Yuren, and Xue Hao, to the Army Prison, where they suffered all kinds of pain. The families of the prisoners jointly accused Ding Lei and requested the Ministry of Justice and the Provincial Party Headquarters to thoroughly investigate and handle the matter. After receiving the accusation, the Ministry of Justice sent Deputy Minister Xie Yingzhou to Suzhou on the 20th to personally investigate the Third Sub-Prison and to question Chief Judge Lin at the High Court. He completed the investigation yesterday (the 21st) and returned to Nanjing that evening. Furthermore, Lawyers Liu Zuwang and Jiang Yiping of the Shanghai Lawyers Association also submitted a telegram to Chief Judge Lin of the High Court on the 20th, requesting that Ding Lei be dismissed and investigated and that all the prisoners transferred to the military prison be returned to the Third Sub-Prison, as they had received repeated requests from the families of the prisoners to protect the rights of those in custody. After receiving the telegram, Chief Judge Lin sent it to the presiding judges of each criminal court to discuss the matter and then make a decision.

Wuxi 74

Provincial Mobile Lecture Team Arrives in Wuxi: The Jiangsu Provincial Party Headquarters organized a mobile lecture team, dividing it into two teams. The first team departed for the 28 counties in Jiangnan to conduct public propaganda. After departing on the 28th of last month, it has been warmly welcomed by the people everywhere. The team completed its propaganda work in counties such as Chuansha, Fengxian, Nanhui, and Songjiang, and arrived in Wuxi yesterday. The county propaganda department has actively prepared to hold a meeting in the auditorium of the Provincial Wuxi High School, and various schools will participate in recreational activities to increase audience interest. A notice has been sent to all sectors of society, inviting them to participate enthusiastically at that time.

Request to Investigate the Arsonist: Xu, a farmer from Xuxiang, near Zhangjing Bridge, Seventh District, Huai Township, is a carpenter by trade. He recently had a quarrel with his aunt, Guo. In anger, he set fire to Guo's house. After neighbors shouted for help and put out the fire, more than six houses were burned down, causing losses of more than 7,000 yuan. Yesterday, the district office reported the case to the county government for investigation.

First Batch of Wounded Soldiers Arrives in Wuxi: At about 5:00 AM yesterday (the 21st), the first batch of thirty to forty wounded soldiers arrived in Wuxi by train from Nanjing. After getting off the train, the wounded soldiers were greeted at the station and escorted to the Huishan Twenty-Second Rear Hospital for recuperation and treatment by personnel from the wounded soldiers reception center and the county government's public security bureau police detachment. County Magistrate Sun issued an official letter to all armed agencies ordering them to comply with the regulations to maintain local order in the areas where the wounded soldiers are stationed.

Black-Clad Bandits Rob Solitary Traveler: Xu Jinshu, the village deputy of Sujiacun, near Beizhu Town on the border of Wuxi and Cheng, was returning home from a wedding banquet in Beizhu Town at about 9:00 PM the day before yesterday. Unexpectedly, when he reached the Huluduantou area less than ten steps from the town, he was suddenly stopped by several bandits dressed in black, speaking with a northern accent. They brandished weapons, forbade him to speak, and searched his entire body. He was robbed of seven yuan in cash, but the thirty-six yuan in banknotes were not taken, which can be considered fortunate.

Organization of a Rice Scarcity Relief Association: Since the beginning of spring, the price of rice in this county has gradually soared, causing panic among the general public. In recent days, due to the small amount of goods arriving and the depletion of stocks, the price of rice has increased sharply. However, unscrupulous merchants who seek profit are still secretly smuggling large quantities of rice out of the country in the hope of making huge profits. The price of high-quality white rice was 18 yuan the day before yesterday, and it rose sharply by seven corners yesterday. Tang Weizhi, a local resident, advocated organizing a rice scarcity relief association to properly plan emergency measures to address the root causes, given the daily rise in rice prices and the hardship of people's lives. He requested that fair merchants from Shanghai, together with fair merchants from the mainland and fair rice merchants from various places, organize it. All public funds accumulated from grain in various counties should be investigated and allocated, and those without cash should be handled separately for fair price sales and rotated on time until the new rice is harvested. If the above methods cannot be implemented in cooperation for the time being, please organize them separately in each county and gradually promote them. All farmers' banks in various places are established to facilitate farmers, and this matter should also imitate the social granary law, purchasing rice and lending it to farmers, and then repaying it at cost. It is hoped that people from all places will quickly join forces to plan and maintain, so that both people's food and security will benefit.

Jiangyin 75

Kidnapping Case Occurs at Zhanwen Bridge: Miao Shouzheng of Zhanwen Bridge, Danan Township, twenty miles outside the east gate, was playing mahjong with friends on the night before last (the 19th) during a heavy rain when four bandits suddenly broke in over the wall and demanded 2,000 yuan in silver. Unsatisfied with what they received, they kidnapped Miao. Someone wanted to report to the defense corps, but there were more than ten bandits outside the door, so they dared not go out and listened as they went west. Afterwards, the defense corps pursued them to the south of Zhangqi Mountain, but found no trace of the bandits. This is the second kidnapping case in Jiangyin since the case at Wangjia Dai to Renji.

Judge Yang Interrogates Harboring Bandits: The Zhouzhuang Defense Corps went to Xiaobaifeng Village the day before yesterday to search for the notorious bandit Lu Zhanglin but failed to find him. They arrested the bandit Zhu Ruikun and Li Ruren, who was harboring the bandit and whose own daughter Li Zhangdi was raped. They were sent to the county the night before last, and yesterday (the 20th) afternoon, Judge Yang interrogated them in the inner court. According to Li Ruren, Lu Zhanglin had come several times from April to the present, and I was forced by his power, so I dared not report him. Li Zhangdi, 23 years old, testified that she had been betrothed to Xu Yongjiang of Zhongjia Alley two years ago. After entering the door, she divorced last year. In April of this year, Xiaogufu Liu Laowu came to my house with Lu Zhanglin and took a fancy to me. On the 20th of this month, Lu came with Qin Qirong and Wang Ziming and forced me to sleep with him. Because I was afraid of his gun, I was raped against my will, and I did not want to. Lu said to my father that he could take me as a concubine and promised my father 1,000 yuan, but my father did not want it either. On the day the defense corps came to arrest him, Lu heard the dogs barking and climbed up to the attic and fired a gun. After the corps members retreated, Lu escaped from the back door, etc. Zhu Ruikun testified that he was from Sanguanxinjing Bridge, a tailor by trade, making clothes in Yi's house and not a bandit. The rest of his testimony was evasive. After the interrogation, he ordered them to be taken into custody together for investigation and handling.

Zhenjiang 76

Zhenjiang Hears of Banditry in Yancheng: According to those who came to the province from Yancheng, the bandit situation in Yancheng has become increasingly rampant in recent days. Various towns and villages along the Binda Longitudinal Lake, such as Shajiazhuang, Linshangzhuang, Shuchengzhuang, Jiangying Town, Feijia Tuan, Anfeng Town, Luohubao, Meisongzhuang, Jianhekou, and Sheyang Town bordering Baoying, and Majiadang Qinggou and other places bordering Funing, have been repeatedly occupied, plundered, burned, killed, and raped by bandits, who have done everything imaginable. Nearly a hundred people have been kidnapped for ransom one after another. Civilian guns have been almost completely seized. In other areas such as Dagang Town in the south of the county, Nanbeiyang in the east of the county, Xinhe Temple Zhenggou in the west of the county, and Genkou in the north of the county, the situation of being robbed and plundered is no less than that of Xidang. There is almost no intact land in the entire county. At this time of busy farming, people cannot make a living, and inland rivers such as Wantai and other ferries have all stopped operating, traffic is cut off, and travel is difficult. If the province does not send heavy troops to thoroughly suppress them, the situation will inevitably spread to Jiangbei. It is hoped that the authorities will plan for this as soon as possible.

Another Banditry Incident in Gaozi: The First Regiment of the National Government Guard Brigade stationed in Zhenjiang received a telegram from Hu Yuanbo, the platoon leader of the Gaozi Station, stating that a gang of bandits had been discovered near the Gaozi Station, and gunfire had been incessant all night. He requested that troops be sent to assist in the defense and suppression. The First Battalion of the Regiment immediately dispatched the machine gun company commander Yuan Zhensheng, leading Platoon Leader Pan Yucheng and a platoon of box soldiers, to the area by small train at about 10:00 AM yesterday to assist in the suppression.

Misfortune for Two People: At 9:00 AM yesterday, the Fifth Train was passing through the Jiuli Temple area at kilometer 230 when a villager, Li Chengming, was resting on the tracks. The train came and he was unable to avoid it, resulting in his head being crushed and killed. Also, at about 4:00 AM, a small train was heading to Jiangkou Station when it reached Xiaozhalankou. A passerby, Zhou Youcai, was passing through the area and was unable to avoid it, resulting in his head being knocked open and his right arm being crushed. His life is in great danger.

Yangzhou 77

Survey Team Causes Misunderstanding Among Villagers: Lin Zhenjia, an engineer from the National Government's Survey Standards Committee Survey Team, and others were surveying the Xinglong'an Yuxu area of Bagangkou in this county on the day before yesterday (the 18th) when a misunderstanding suddenly arose among the villagers along the riverbank, and they beat drums and gathered crowds, intending to use barbarism. The officials tried their best to persuade them and promote the meaning of the survey, and the matter was resolved.

Detective Team Captures Key Robbers of a Ship: The county detective team arrested four bandits, including Hu Dezheng, and seized a pistol at the Huacheng Hotel in Gengzi Street at 3:00 AM yesterday (the 19th). When they were leaving, two people came to visit the Hu bandits. The two people were also taken to the team for questioning. According to their confession, the ship robbery case in Baota Bay and the robbery case in Huojia Bridge were all committed by these bandits. There are still many accomplices hiding in the Xingdong area. It is said that County Magistrate Chen has sent a probe to ask the two counties to help with the joint arrest.

Submitting a Report on the Distribution of Disaster Relief: The Jiangdu Relief Branch sent a letter to the County Consolidation Committee, appointing Bi Yinchen and others to supervise the distribution of disaster relief goods worth ninety taels of silver. The committee has already issued commissions. It has now been determined that they will be divided into three grades: A, six corners per household with the word "Relief," for extremely poor households with five or more people; B, four corners per household with the word "Work," for extremely poor households with fewer than five people or the next poorest with six or more people; C, two corners per household for the next poorest or extremely poor households with only two people. Yesterday (the 19th), the tables were checked and filled out by the county for forwarding to the government, awaiting orders for implementation.

Government Order to Establish a National Goods Market: The county received instructions from the Construction Department to inform the Provincial Commercial Consolidation Committee, which was approved by the provincial government to order all counties to establish national goods markets in order to promote domestic goods. Yesterday (the 19th), the First District Office was specially instructed to cooperate with the County Chamber of Commerce National Goods Exhibition Preparatory Committee to actively prepare.

Qingjiang 78

Provincial Order on Doorplate Fees: The Huaiyin Public Security Bureau previously planned to order city and rural doorplates and collect fees to raise funds for guns and ammunition, and submitted a document to the county government for review and approval. However, the various district offices in this county also needed funds for personnel registration, household census, and other matters, and had similar actions, making it difficult for the county government to handle. Therefore, the matter was forwarded to the Civil Affairs Department for instructions. A provincial order was received, allowing it to be handled within the territory of the First District, while other districts would be handled later. However, before the First District handles it, it should be appraised in accordance with the facts, and the collection procedures, compilation methods, income and expenditure budget, and future protection, relief, construction, and revision should be planned in detail and reported for verification and approval before being implemented. After receiving the order, the county government immediately issued a sub-order to each district office and the Public Security Bureau to comply with the provincial order regarding the reporting and verification. The Public Security Bureau was further instructed to plan in detail beforehand, formulate appropriate measures, and then discuss them at the upcoming district chief meeting before reporting them to the government for verification and approval.

Major Suppression of Bandits in the Nine Counties of Jiangbei: The Provincial Security Office mobilized all twenty companies of the provincial police team, combined with the two infantry battalions under the command of Chief Commander Xiong, and the shallow-water warships of the Wusong Naval Police District to launch a major suppression of bandits and communists in the nine counties of Tong, Ru, and others. Remote ports along the river and sea were all blockaded, and local police teams and defense corps were responsible for searching for ambushed bandits and for water and land transportation. A key communist leader was captured and escaped: The provincial police team captured a key communist leader, Wu Zhanlong, in Tongcheng and sent him to the Second Jia Town Command for interrogation. He confessed without denial. Because he had confessed that there were key criminals in the city, Yu Xigong Security Bureau sent Du Yutian to escort him to the city as an informant. Unexpectedly, he escaped on South Street. The provincial police team is searching for Du.

Relief Agency Scheduled to Be Established: Various charitable organizations in Tongyi will be merged and reorganized into a relief agency. The county government has hired Zong Weichuan, Wu Xuanjie, Feng Guangjiu, and seventeen others as committee members, and it is scheduled to be established early next month.

Strictly Prevent Bandits from Smuggling Arms and Ammunition: The Tongyi military police have repeatedly cracked cases of smuggling military fire in the Tiansheng Renyao ports. According to the confessions of the captured criminals, they were in contact with party members in the Qihai area. Inspections at each port are very strict these days.

Rugao 80

Guerrilla Warfare Between the Yeguantiao Temple Defense Corps and Bandits: On the 16th, the First District Defense Corps received a report that the bandits had surrounded the troops stationed at Shaojiazhuang on three sides. After receiving the report, Commander Ma concentrated the defense corps stationed in various places at the regimental headquarters. At about 11:00 PM that night, he ordered them to depart and go to the Shaojiazhuang area to suppress the bandits. When they arrived at Yeguanti Temple, they suddenly encountered many communists, and the two sides opened fire and made contact. After an hour of fierce fighting, the bandits were unable to resist and retreated. In this battle, two bandits were killed and eighteen were captured alive. The heads of the killed bandits were cut off and sent to the city for public display.

Provincial Police Suppress Bandits in Jiangduo: The Tenth Company of the Provincial Police Team stationed in Jiangduo was ordered on the 11th to go to Chenjiazhuang to suppress the bandits. More than 2,000 bandits took advantage of the emptiness to attack. The guards immediately resisted and fought back. When the main force heard the news, they turned back and surrounded the bandits, who were defeated and fled. More than 100 bandits were killed on the spot, and many guns were seized.

Zhangguzhuang School Burned Down: The Zhangguzhuang Zhang's Private School and Zhang Xiusheng's residence in Rugao Lifaqu were burned down by bandits on the night of the 16th, causing huge losses.

The Chief of the Public Security Bureau, Guan Jing, Extorts Money: Zhou Dingbo, the chief of the Motou District Public Security Branch in this county, abused his power to extort money. He is now being sued by the victims Chen Ziyan and others to the county government. After investigation, it was found to be true. On the afternoon of the 17th, Judge Sun opened a court hearing, and Zhou was still sophistical. Judge Sun ruled that Zhou's extortion of money was conclusive and ordered him to be detained for sentencing and not allowed to be released on bail.

A Large Number of Police Teams Search: County Magistrate Qian and the Chief of the Public Security Bureau led a large number of police teams, more than 100 people, to Rugao High School at about 4:00 AM on the 18th to search. They first surrounded the school, and the sentries along the way were densely deployed and extremely strict. The students were all awakened while still sound asleep. As a result, nothing was found.

Jiashan 81

A Cruel History of Lake Pirates: Yesterday, in the Heshangdang area of Yuyao District, a fishing boat owned by Zhang San and Hu Jinsheng was fishing when they were suddenly encountered by four pirate ships. The pirates, dissatisfied with the small catch, became enraged and tied up Zhang and Hu, brutally beating them. Their wives knelt and pleaded for mercy, but the pirates used fire to burn their breasts and genitals. Subsequently, Hu's young son, A Long, was stabbed in the stomach with a Miao spear for the pirates' amusement. Hu Jinsheng and his wife witnessed this tragic scene and fainted. Before leaving, the pirates kidnapped Zhang's eldest daughter, A Bao.

Hangzhou 82

Active Construction of the Yan-Hui Highway: Chen Ticheng, Director of the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau, regards the Yan-Hui Highway as crucial to Zhejiang Province's transportation. He dispatched engineer Yu Zhewen to lead a team for surveying and determining the route, which runs from Yanzhou to Huizhou, passing through the counties of Fuyang, Xindeng, Fenshui, Jiande, and Chun'an. The road is approximately 300 li long, and construction commenced in mid-March of this year. Over one-third of the entire road has already been completed. Yesterday (the 22nd), the Bureau, in order to expedite the project and ensure its opening to traffic in the autumn of this year, urged the Construction Department to forward a letter to the Finance Department requesting the allocation of funds for the project. They also dispatched personnel for inspection.

Shaoxing 83

Provincial Order to Reduce Slaughter Tax Assessment: After the previous contractor for the Shaoxing slaughter tax suffered losses and withdrew, the county re-tendered the contract. As no one bid, County Magistrate Tang requested the Finance Department to reduce the minimum bid amount. An order has now been received approving a reduction to 28,000 yuan as the lowest bid, and the re-tendering will take place on the 23rd.

Petition to Investigate the Junde School: The County Party Department recently investigated the privately-run Junde Girls' School and found that it was oppressing students, forcing them to attend religious services, and punishing them for refusal. This constitutes religious aggression and violates the Party and the nation to an extreme degree. On the 19th, the committee resolved to petition the Provincial Party Department to forward a letter to the Education Department for investigation and handling.

New Finance Bureau Chief to Take Office on Schedule: Wu Zeyi, Chief of the Shaoxing Finance Bureau, has been ordered to transfer to the province. The vacant position will be filled by Ling Pu, who is scheduled to arrive in Shaoxing on the 26th to take office.

Education News

Important News: Ministry of Education Order

Submit Rosters of Graduates from All Schools 85

The Ministry of Education issued an order to all provincial education departments to submit rosters of graduates from all schools. The order reads:

The rosters of graduates from schools at all levels are of utmost importance for examining student qualifications. Students' admission to higher education, lawyer qualifications, doctor certifications, civil service examinations, and other matters often encounter difficulties due to qualification issues. Although the Ministry retains archives from the former Qing Dynasty Ministry of Education and the former Beijing Ministry of Education, which are sufficient for reference, the numerous volumes may have omissions. Therefore, a separate investigation should be conducted for verification purposes. In addition to issuing separate instructions, this order directs your department to investigate and submit rosters of graduates from all public and registered private secondary and higher education institutions within your jurisdiction, according to the format provided below. Alternatively, you may instruct each school to report in detail and submit the information to your department for compilation and forwarding to the Ministry for verification. This order includes the following nine items: (1) Name; (2) Gender; (3) Native place; (4) Department; (5) Class; (6) Graduation performance; (7) Graduation date; (8) Approving authority and date; (9) Remarks.

Guangdong Construction Department Promotes Waterborne Education 86

To Obtain Excellent Seamen and Sailors,

Attention Must First Be Paid to the Education of Tankas

(Guangzhou Correspondent) Deng Yanhua, Director of the Guangdong Construction Department, recently stated that the Tankas (boat people) living along the water are fellow citizens, yet they are almost like foreigners. Moreover, many drivers and sailors come from Tanka families. If they do not receive proper education, it will greatly affect the future of the nation. Yesterday (the 10th), he submitted a memorial to the provincial government requesting that the Education Department be instructed to pay attention to Tanka education. The original memorial reads: "Regarding the matter of submitting a petition, it is noted that Guangdong Province has numerous rivers and ports, and the shipping business is increasing daily. Consequently, the number of Tankas is also growing. Those of lower quality are familiar with water and skilled in handling boats. Those of average quality have some knowledge of shipping routes and specialize in piloting. Generally, they are crude by nature, live by the sea, and are difficult to manage and educate. Therefore, government agencies often let them be, resulting in the waterfront being almost like a foreign land. However, it is crucial to recognize that Guangdong Province is both a major trading area and a naval base. Many ship drivers and naval sailors come from Tanka families. If the foundation is poor, the results will be greatly affected. Seamen cannot compete with foreigners at sea, and sailors cannot serve the country effectively. Therefore, to obtain excellent seamen and sailors, attention must first be paid to the education of the Tanka people. However, navigation affairs are under the jurisdiction of the Construction Department, while education is the responsibility of the Education Department. To implement waterborne education, this document is submitted to your office, requesting that the Education Department be instructed to pay attention to the education of the Tanka people, so that they are not left out. Furthermore, please investigate the situation and promote waterborne schools to achieve universal education and cultivate talent. Whether this is appropriate is left for your wise decision. (June 12th)"

May 5th Designated as a Holiday 87

Whether May 5th, the anniversary of the Premier assuming the extraordinary presidency, is a holiday was not specified in the academic calendar. Therefore, this year, educational institutions and schools only received notification from the central government and the Party headquarters in the morning of that day, and only then took a day off. The Ministry of Education previously petitioned the Executive Yuan for an interpretation as to whether May 5th should be designated as a regular holiday. The Executive Yuan submitted a report to the government, which was approved by the central government. Henceforth, May 5th will be officially a holiday for commemoration.

Ministry of Education Issues Circular on World Cooperation Day 88

The Ministry of Education issued a circular to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities stating that the first Saturday of July this year is World Cooperation Day. The circular reads: "Following the instructions of the Executive Yuan, which approved a letter from the Propaganda Department of the Central Executive Committee stating that the cooperative movement is one of the seven movements stipulated by the Central Government and should be widely promoted, it is hereby decided that starting on the first Saturday of July this year (World Cooperation Day), the propaganda departments of the Party headquarters in all provinces and special municipalities shall, together with the local provincial and municipal governments, organize cooperative movement propaganda groups. The propaganda departments of the provincial Party headquarters shall also instruct the Party headquarters in all counties and cities to hold similar events simultaneously in conjunction with the local county and municipal governments to promote the movement. In addition to reporting and issuing separate instructions, this circular directs your department/bureau to comply immediately and instruct all subordinates to comply as well."

Ministry of Education Strictly Orders Destruction of Classical Chinese Textbook Plates 91

The Ministry of Education is sparing no effort in banning textbooks in classical Chinese. Previously, the Shanghai Special Municipal Education Bureau reported the results of its investigation into the issuance of elementary school textbooks in classical Chinese by various bookstores and instructed the bureau that, despite the bookstores claiming to have no remaining stock and having ceased distribution, books in classical Chinese from Zhonghua, Shijie, Shangwu, and Guomin bookstores could still be purchased when the Ministry sent people to Beijing. This showed that the bookstores' claims of having no remaining stock and having voluntarily stopped selling were lies. The bureau should be instructed to warn them. As for the printing aspect, since all the bookstores claimed to have stopped printing, all the stone printing templates and paper boards for various elementary school textbooks in classical Chinese have become waste. To prevent further unauthorized printing, the education bureau should promptly send personnel to inspect them one by one, seal them all up, and submit a detailed list to the Ministry so that it can send personnel to supervise their destruction or transport them to designated museums, educational halls, and other places for display. The above points should be complied with and a report submitted promptly. Subsequently, the bureau requested a change to the method of banning elementary school textbooks in classical Chinese for the Shanghai Shangwu Library, and a temporary delay in the destruction of paper molds and printing plates was approved. The Ministry instructed that this should not be discussed and simultaneously instructed the education departments of the three northeastern provinces, Guangdong, and Fujian to instruct primary schools not to use textbooks in classical Chinese thereafter. The two orders are recorded below.

Instructions to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau 92

Your report has been noted. This Ministry, in order to ban elementary school textbooks in classical Chinese, issued a circular to seal up the paper molds and printing plates of these books. All bookstores have complied. The library should not be unique. The vernacular textbooks for elementary schools in the three northeastern provinces and Guangdong and Fujian provinces are also widely used. If a small number of schools still use elementary school textbooks in classical Chinese privately, the local education authorities have not provided sufficient guidance and should be instructed by this Ministry to earnestly provide guidance and prohibit them. Although the situation in Nanyang (Southeast Asia) is different, most important locations such as Singapore, the Philippines, and Java use vernacular textbooks. For those who stubbornly insist on using elementary school textbooks in classical Chinese, the Ministry should still instruct the consuls and consult with the Central Propaganda Department to instruct the Party branches at all levels overseas to provide guidance and prohibit them, so as to thoroughly implement this Ministry's plan to ban elementary school textbooks in classical Chinese. The Shanghai Library's request for a temporary postponement of the sealing up of paper molds and printing plates for elementary school textbooks in classical Chinese should not be discussed. In addition to instructing the education departments of the three northeastern provinces, Fujian, and Guangdong, and the consuls stationed abroad, and consulting with the Central Propaganda Department, this order directs your bureau to instruct the library to acknowledge this.

Order to the Education Departments of the Three Northeastern Provinces, Guangdong, and Fujian 93

This Ministry, in order to ban elementary school textbooks in classical Chinese, previously issued a circular to all provincial and municipal education administrative organs, instructing all bookstores to seal up all paper molds and printing plates of these books. Now, the Shanghai bookstores report that the three northeastern provinces and Fujian and Guangdong provinces still use elementary school textbooks in classical Chinese and request permission to temporarily postpone the sealing up of these paper molds and printing plates to alleviate the difficulties of the merchants. This Ministry has found that vernacular textbooks for elementary schools have long been in circulation in these provinces. Why are there still schools using classical Chinese textbooks? If this is the case, it is due to lax enforcement and insufficient guidance. This order directs you to instruct all primary schools under your jurisdiction not to use classical Chinese textbooks thereafter in order to promote education and emphasize decrees. In addition to instructing the bookstores that their request should not be discussed and issuing separate instructions, this order directs you to comply and not delay.

The Jiangsu Provincial Teacher Certification Committee for Party Principles, considering that the two-year validity period of the previously certified teachers of Party principles is about to expire, and in order to alleviate the shortage of talent, submitted a request to the central government and the Ministry of Education to extend the validity period. Zhejiang Education Department

Subsidizing the High School Expenses of Zhejiang University 95

Provincial Funds to Be Allocated from 1930 Onward for Maintenance

Five Articles Establishing Methods for Subsidizing Expenses

The Zhejiang Education Department believes that the establishment of high schools affiliated with the Agricultural and Engineering Colleges of Zhejiang University hinders the university's own development. It has decided to cease enrollment starting in 1930 and close them down gradually. The department believes that this reduces the opportunity to cultivate practical talents, which is contrary to the needs of industrial education in the province and the resolutions of the National Education Conference. Therefore, it has drafted a proposal and established five articles for subsidizing expenses, which were submitted to the provincial government for review. The proposal was approved by the 319th committee meeting yesterday. The original text of the proposal is as follows: The chairman has successively received a document from Gu Yuxiu, professor of the Engineering College of National Zhejiang University, stating four reasons why the industrial program of the high school affiliated with the Engineering College should not be stopped immediately, and requesting that a way be found to maintain it. Also received was a document from Liu Dexiang, a graduate of the former Zhejiang Provincial Class A Industrial School, stating that the industrial school has been operating successfully and requesting that a way be found to maintain it if it is to be closed down. The chairman instructed the Education Department to review and respond. Zhejiang University also sent a letter stating that the high-level industrial high school affiliated with the Engineering College and the high-level agricultural high school affiliated with the Agricultural College have been operating for many years with considerable success. However, the university's funding is insufficient, and the affiliated high schools require significant expenses, which hinder the university's own development. The colleges have been instructed to cease enrollment and close down gradually starting in 1930. The Engineering College has submitted a report stating that it has complied with the order to cease enrollment and close down gradually, and has submitted five Su Miqian's leveling instruments, which were transferred by the former principal of the Engineering College, for verification and cancellation. Please verify and respond. The high-level agricultural and industrial high schools affiliated with the Agricultural and Engineering Colleges of Zhejiang University were originally vocational schools affiliated with the Zhejiang Provincial Public Agricultural and Industrial Specialized Schools. When the agricultural and industrial specialized schools were reorganized into the Agricultural and Engineering Colleges of National Zhejiang University, the affiliated vocational schools were also reorganized into affiliated high-level high schools. Now, Zhejiang University, due to funding issues, will stop enrolling new students in the affiliated high schools in 1930, which means that Zhejiang will have one less institution for cultivating practical talents. Industrial education in Zhejiang is not well-developed. There are still no provincial agricultural and industrial schools. There are only Ningbo Municipal Industrial High School and Qu County and Jiangshan Private Agricultural Vocational Schools among the city and county private vocational schools. Agricultural and industrial schools cannot be compared to ordinary schools. Their farms, factories, and laboratories require various equipment that cannot be set up and perfected overnight. The former provincial agricultural and industrial schools have been operating for more than ten years before they can achieve some success. The society has a great need for agricultural and industrial talents, as evidenced by the situation of graduates from these schools in the past. If the high schools affiliated with the Agricultural and Engineering Colleges of Zhejiang University are closed down, there will be a sudden shortage of such talents, which will not be enough to meet the actual needs of society. Furthermore, the "Improvement Plan for National Education," resolved at the Second National Education Conference, called for the separate establishment of more agricultural and industrial high schools during the period of political tutelage, or the conversion of ordinary high schools. Due to financial constraints, this province has not been able to plan for this this year. However, it is necessary to continue to maintain the existing agricultural and industrial high schools affiliated with the Agricultural and Engineering Colleges of Zhejiang University. Based on the above reasons, five articles for subsidizing the expenses of the high schools affiliated with the Agricultural and Engineering Colleges of Zhejiang University are proposed as follows: (1) It is requested that the high schools affiliated with the Agricultural and Engineering Colleges of Zhejiang University continue to enroll new students starting in 1930. (2) The high schools affiliated with the Agricultural and Engineering Colleges of Zhejiang University will be subsidized by the Zhejiang Provincial Government at a rate of 4,000 silver dollars per class per year for the new students enrolled after 1930, based on the number of classes, and paid monthly from the provincial treasury. However, each class of new students must have at least 20 students. Those with fewer than 20 students will be placed in other departments and will not be opened as separate classes. (3) The Agricultural and Engineering Colleges of Zhejiang University should report the number of new students and new classes established in each affiliated high school to the Zhejiang Provincial Education Department at the beginning of each academic year. (4) The Agricultural and Engineering Colleges of Zhejiang University should report the income and expenditure of the regular and temporary expenses of the affiliated high schools to the Zhejiang Provincial Education Department for reference at the end of each semester. (5) The Zhejiang Provincial Education Department should send personnel to inspect the high schools affiliated with the Agricultural and Engineering Colleges of Zhejiang University at least twice each semester and report the results of the inspection to the provincial government. Whether the above measures are feasible is submitted for public deliberation.

Faculty and Staff of Labor University Host Banquet for Academic Community 101

The entire faculty and staff of the National Labor University are extremely indignant at the Ministry of Education's sudden order to halt enrollment at the university and undermine labor education, which is a bizarre event. They have repeatedly elected representatives to host members of the press from Beijing and Shanghai to announce the true facts and oppose the Ministry of Education, as previously reported. Last night, they also hosted a banquet for prominent members of the Shanghai academic community at the Hua An Building. Attendees included He Bingsong, Jiang Wenyu, Zheng Hongnian, Dong Renjian, Zheng Tonghe, and Jin Wensi. During the banquet, the guests and hosts exchanged opinions. Xiong Renan and others from the faculty and staff of Labor University put forward four key points: (1) The Ministry of Education has always specialized in undermining university education institutions without providing assistance. The order to halt enrollment at Labor University without cause is just one example. (2) Labor University is the highest institution of labor education in the country and has the mission of cultivating specialized talents and developing agricultural and industrial education. The Ministry of Education has not only never provided guidance but has also blamed the university for "labor not being associated with universities," showing that the Ministry of Education does not understand the meaning of labor education. (3) Labor University currently has more than a thousand students, mostly from poor classes who are hardworking, resilient, diligent, and eager to learn. The Ministry of Education's action is tantamount to depriving these young people of the opportunity to study and treating university education as the exclusive property of the capitalist class. (4) The Ministry of Education's personnel sent to inspect the school had preconceived notions. Therefore, they did not hesitate to fabricate charges to achieve their plan to destroy Labor University. All the guests believed that the Ministry of Education's handling was inappropriate and expressed deep sympathy for the school. They also expressed their willingness to uphold justice and provide appropriate assistance.

Record of the General Affairs Section Meeting of the County Education Bureau 105

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held its 61st General Affairs Section meeting the day before yesterday afternoon at 1 p.m. Nine people attended, with Director Shi presiding. The agenda included: (1) Rituals were performed as usual; (2) A report was given on the progress of the section's work last week; (3) Discussion. (1) Regarding how to prepare the 18th-year final accounts, it was decided that the following procedures should be submitted to the Bureau Affairs Meeting for approval and implementation: (A) First, the actual figures for the bureau's revenue and expenditure statement should be finalized by July 10; (B) The bureau's administrative and operational expenses and special expenses should be compiled by the accounting section by July 15; (C) The bureau will order all county schools and social education institutions to prepare final accounts, along with all receipts, and report them to the bureau by July 17; (D) The educational expenses handled by the district offices should be based on the resolution of the bureau's district talks, and the education committees and district chiefs should prepare final accounts and report them to the bureau by July 15; (E) The format of the final accounts will be printed and distributed by the bureau. (2) Regarding the division of ordinary accounting and special accounting, it was decided that the principle would be adopted, and the accounting section would propose a division of items for discussion at the Bureau Affairs Meeting. (3) Regarding the addition of three items to ordinary accounting, it was decided that the proposal would be approved and implemented from July 19th, with the addition of the following subjects: "Administration," "General Education," "Free Education," "Social Education," "Special Expenses." (4) Regarding whether to inquire with the Property Management Office about the missing land lease contract for Gu Yizhi's rented land, which was transferred to the bureau in January of the 18th year, it was decided to send an inquiry.

Great China University Adds Kindergarten Normal School 106

Great China University, recognizing the importance of kindergarten education in our country and the lack of kindergarten teachers, will add a Women's Kindergarten Normal School and an affiliated kindergarten at the new campus on Fanwangdu Zhongshan Road this autumn to facilitate teaching and learning. Educational psychology experts Chen Heqin, Ou Yuanhuai, Lu Jizeng, Chen Xuan, Shan, Huang Jingsi, Zhang Yaoxiang, Dong Renjian, and Yang Baokang were hired to form a steering committee to plan the entire facility. All courses and equipment are striving for perfection, and Ms. Yang Baokang has been appointed as the director of the school. Ms. Yang has a bachelor's degree from Wellesley College in the United States and a master's degree from Columbia University, specializing in kindergarten education. She has served as a professor at Datong University and the principal of Jiangsu Provincial Nanjing Women's Middle School, where she founded a kindergarten teacher training institute and the Nanjing Central Kindergarten. She has extensive knowledge and experience in kindergarten education. The school will hold entrance examinations for new students on July 14th and 15th. Any woman with a junior high school diploma or above can apply.

International Track and Field Events 111

Point Scoring Method Determined

Records Set With the Wind To Be Retained

The World News Agency reports that the International Sports Committee, due to the tenth International Sports Games to be held in Los Angeles, USA, in two years, first met in Berlin on May 25, with representatives from 54 countries attending to discuss the matter. (Track Events) 100 meters, 200 meters, 400 meters, 800 meters, 1,500 meters, 5,000 meters, 110-meter hurdles, 400-meter hurdles, relay (400 meters, 300 meters, 200 meters, 100 meters); (Field Events) Long jump, high jump, pole vault, javelin throw, discus throw; (Point Scoring Method) 5, 3, 1, 0.
